---
layout: lexeme
lexeme: Maatunut

###  Maatunut₁

* _This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Maatunut* (composted)_
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  47
* Origins: finer 
* Possible NER class:  GEO
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
